```c
#include <stdio.h>

void printBinary(int n) {
    int binary[32], i = 0;
    while (n) {
        binary[i++] = n & 1;
        n >>= 1;
    }
    while (i--) {
        printf("%d", binary[i]);
    }
}

int main() {
    int num;
    printf("Enter a decimal number: ");
    scanf("%d", &num);
    printf("Binary equivalent: ");
    printBinary(num);
    return 0;
}
```

```c
#include <stdio.h>

void printBinary(int n) {
    int binary[32], i = 0;
    while (n) {
        binary[i++] = n & 1;
        n >>= 1;
    }
    while (i--) {
        printf("%d", binary[i]);
    }
}

int main() {
    int num;
    printf("Enter a decimal number: ");
    scanf("%d", &num);
    printf("Binary equivalent: ");
    printBinary(num);
    return 0;
}
```
